## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Test Suite] --> B{Test Type}
    B -->|Validation Tests| C[test_solution_id_as_int_value]
    B -->|Validation Tests| D[test_old_state_as_bad_value]
    B -->|Validation Tests| E[test_new_state_as_bad_value]
    B -->|Validation Tests| F[test_changed_by_as_bad_value]
    B -->|CRUD Tests| G[test_container_lifecycle_state_create]
    B -->|CRUD Tests| H[test_container_lifecycle_state_read]
    B -->|CRUD Tests| I[test_container_lifecycle_state_update]
    B -->|CRUD Tests| J[test_container_lifecycle_state_delete]
    C --> K[Assert Raises AssertionError]
    D --> K
    E --> K
    F --> K
    G --> L[Create Row in DB]
    H --> M[Read Row from DB]
    I --> N[Update Row in DB]
    J --> O[Delete Row from DB]
    K --> P[End Test]
    L --> P
    M --> P
    N --> P
    O --> P
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as ContainerLifeCycleStateTest
    participant CRUD as CrudOperations
    participant Model as PackageContainerLifecycleHistory
    participant DB as Database Connector
    Test->>Model: Create instance from_dict(json)
    Test->>CRUD: create_row(connector, table, columns, model)
    CRUD->>DB: Insert data
    DB-->>CRUD: Return result
    CRUD-->>Test: Return created object
    Test->>Model: Create instance with id
    Test->>CRUD: read(connector, table, columns, model)
    CRUD->>DB: Query by id
    DB-->>CRUD: Return data
    CRUD-->>Test: Return object
    Test->>Model: set(new_state, value)
    Test->>CRUD: update_row(connector, table, columns, model)
    CRUD->>DB: Update data
    DB-->>CRUD: Return result
    CRUD-->>Test: Return updated object
    Test->>CRUD: delete(connector, table, columns, model)
    CRUD->>DB: Soft delete
    DB-->>CRUD: Return result
    CRUD-->>Test: Return deleted object
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> OLD_STATE
    OLD_STATE --> NEW_STATE: changed_event
    NEW_STATE --> NEW_STATE_UPDATE: update operation
    NEW_STATE_UPDATE --> DELETED: delete operation
    DELETED --> [*]
    note right of OLD_STATE
        Initial state of container
    end note
    note right of NEW_STATE
        Updated state via lifecycle event
    end note
    note right of DELETED
        Soft deleted state
    end note
```
